to clipboard" class="button button--variant_ghost button--size_sm px_0 d_none lg:d_inline-flex c_gray.dark.12 hover:bg_gray.dark.a3"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" [&amp;_&gt;_pre]:p_4 scroller"><pre style="padding:var(--spacing-4);margin:0;color:var(--colors-gray-dark-11)"><code>import { Slider } from &#x27;@ark-ui/react/slider&#x27;
import styles from &#x27;./index.module.css&#x27;

export const Basic = () =&gt; {
  return (
    &lt;Slider.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue={[40]}&gt;
      &lt;div style={{ display: &#x27;flex&#x27;, justifyContent: &#x27;space-between&#x27; }}&gt;
        &lt;Slider.Label className={styles.Label}&gt;Label&lt;/Slider.Label&gt;
        &lt;Slider.ValueText className={styles.ValueText} /&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;Slider.Control className={styles.Control}&gt;
        &lt;Slider.Track className={styles.Track}&gt;
          &lt;Slider.Range className={styles.Range} /&gt;
        &lt;/Slider.Track&gt;
        &lt;Slider.Thumb index={0} className={styles.Thumb}&gt;
          &lt;Slider.HiddenInput /&gt;
        &lt;/Slider.Thumb&gt;
      &lt;/Slider.Control&gt;
    &lt;/Slider.Root&gt;
  )
}
</code></pre></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="d_flex flex-d_row gap_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center jc_center flex_0_0_auto w_8 h_8 bdr_9999px c_fg.default bg_bg.default bd-w_1px z_1 bx-sh_0_0_0_12px_var(--colors-bg-surface) fw_semibold">4</div><h3 class="text text--variant_heading my_0! textStyle_xl">Style a component</h3></div><div class="ps_12 [&amp;&gt;_:last-child]:mb_0"><p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Ark UI is a headless component library that doesn&#x27;t include default styles.
You can leverage the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-scope</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-part</code> attributes to style your components with custom CSS.</p><p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">For example, to style a slider component, you can target its parts using these attributes:</p><pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">/* Targets the &lt;Slider.Root /&gt; */</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-scope</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;slider&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">][</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-part</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;root&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  display</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">flex</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  flex-direction</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">column</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre><p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Check out the <a href="/react/docs/guides/styling" class="link">Styling Components guide</a> to learn more about styling components in Ark UI.</p></div></div><div class=""><div class="d_flex flex-d_row gap_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center jc_center flex_0_0_auto w_8 h_8 bdr_9999px c_fg.default bg_bg.default bd-w_1px z_1 bx-sh_0_0_0_12px_var(--colors-bg-surface) fw_semibold">5</div><h3 class="text text--variant_heading my_0! textStyle_xl">That&#x27;s it</h3></div><div class="ps_12 [&amp;&gt;_:last-child]:mb_0"><p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Congratulations! You&#x27;ve successfully set up and styled your components using Ark UI. If you run into any issues or have
questions, open an issue on our <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://github.com/chakra-ui/ark/issues/new/choose" class="link">GitHub</a> or reach out on
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://discord.gg/ww6HE5xaZ2" class="link">Discord</a>.</p><p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline
